`remotecache.Register(CacheableStruct{})`\ntype CacheStorage interface {\n\t// Get gets the cache value as an byte array\n\tGet(ctx context.Context, key string) ([]byte, error)\n\n\t// Set saves the It provides `HandleQueryRequest()` and `HandleResourceRequest()` methods that check the cache and return `CachedQueryDataResponse` objects containing both the cached response and an update function. The middleware also implements request deduplication via `requestDeduplicationMiddleware` when the `FlagQueryCacheRequestDeduplication` feature is enabled. Metrics are collected in **caching_metrics.go** tracking query caching request durations and cache hit/miss rates.\\n\\n## 3. Cache Backend Abstraction\\n\\nThe cache backend is abstracted through the `CacheStorage` interface in **pkg/infra/remotecache/remotecache.go**. Multiple backend implementations are supported:\\n\\n- **redis_storage.go**: Redis backend using go-redis client with configurable connection strings\\n- **memcached_storage.go**: Memcached backend using the gomemcache library\\n- **database_storage.go**: Database backend using SQL with the `cache_data` table, including automatic garbage collection of expired entries\\n- **pkg/infra/localcache/cache.go**: In-memory local cache using the go-cache library with default 5-minute expiration\\n\\nEach backend supports TTL-based expiration with a default maximum of 24 hours if not specified.\\n\\n## 4. The `DashboardSaved()` method in the DashboardHandler publishes dashboard change events to the GitOps channel and dashboard-specific channels. This event can trigger cache invalidation in listening services.\\n\\nAdditional cache control mechanisms include:\\n- **Skip Query Cache Header**: The middleware checks for `X-Cache-Skip: true` header in **pkg/middleware/middleware.go** and sets `SkipQueryCache` flag in the request context\\n- **Request Context**: **pkg/services/contexthandler/model/model.go** includes the `SkipQueryCache` boolean field for per-request cache bypass\\n\\n## 6.
